     edit
     QubeTX Landing ‚ÄĒ Full Redesign Plan (v3.0.0)

     Context

     The current qubetx.com landing page (Next.js 16 + React 19 + Tailwind v4 +
     CSS Modules, static export ‚Üí GitHub Pages) gets a ground-up redesign.
     Drivers:

     1. The hero/header mockup image: deep navy-black, heavy condensed 3-line
     headline ("SOLID CODE. / STRONGER SYSTEMS. / LIMITLESS POSSIBILITIES." ‚ÄĒ
     last line blue‚Üípurple gradient), mono eyebrow + bordered mono subtitle,
     outlined GET STARTED ‚Üí button, "EXPLORE OUR SERVICES ‚†Ņ" link, bottom-left
     cube + "A DEPARTMENT OF ES DEVELOPMENT LLC", right-side dot-matrix field
     growing/brightening toward bottom-right, centered mono nav (SERVICES ‚Ėĺ,
     TECHNOLOGIES, ABOUT US, WORK, CONTACT).
     2. Visual standards from qube-machine-report-homepage (tokens,
     cubic-bezier(0.25,1,0.5,1) easing, mono label pills, striped rows,
     version-badge chips, grid-cell sections, terminal aesthetic) ‚ÄĒ applied to
     the current architecture (TS + CSS Modules + vitest + Pretext stay).
     3. Heavy motion: anime.js v4 + Framer Motion. The hero dot grid is fully 
     anime.js-driven and interactive. A scroll-scrubbed background draws forward
     going down and reverses going up. Custom cursor keeps its look, rebuilt
     properly. Interaction character: design.cash.app ("intentional, effortless,
     organic" ‚ÄĒ punchy springs, slide-up/sequenced type, physical reactions).
     4. The site is itself the portfolio piece ‚ÄĒ it must demonstrate the
     design/engineering attention to detail QubeTX sells. Micro-interactions for
     discoverability; Easter eggs themed to the business
     (diagnostics/terminal/cube/dots).
     5. Dedicated Products section for the product line (TR-300, SD-300, ND-300,
     WB-300, shaughvOS ‚Üí reports.qubetx.com); "System Reports" removed from the
     Work grid (dedup).
     6. Fonts: local Makira Sans (modern grotesk w/ ink traps; Black weight
     carries the headline) + IBM Plex Mono, copied into the repo from
     C:\Users\hey\Documents\NEWFONTS2026\{Makira-Sans-Serif,IBM-Plex-Mono}\Web\
     (woff2), via next/font/local. Unbounded/Space Grotesk/Space Mono retired.

     Verified codebase facts (audited by me, not just subagents)

     - PretextProvider.tsx:24-28 gates readiness on literal '16px 
     Unbounded'-style names ‚ÄĒ can never pass under next/font's rewritten family 
     names, so Pretext always burns its full 3s fallback today. Must be fixed
     with the font swap. PretextBlock itself is safe (reads getComputedStyle).
     - CI (.github/workflows/ci.yml) runs lint + build only ‚ÄĒ no tests. Add npm 
     test.
     - src/test/setup.ts auto-mocks only @/lib/pretext; framer-motion is mocked
     per-file from src/test/mocks/framer-motion.ts. Promote FM mock to setup.ts;
     add animejs mock.
     - globals.css:78 scroll-behavior: smooth fights Lenis ‚Üí remove.
     globals.css:215 global 44px min-width/min-height on all a, button would
     wreck compact mono nav links ‚Üí scope to content/padding-based hit areas.
     - Current Header has no nav (logo + skip link only) ‚ÄĒ new header is a fresh
     build.
     - app/wallpaper/page.tsx uses R3F WallpaperMatrix ‚ÄĒ leave untouched;
     three/@react-three/* stay installed even though the index route drops them
     (~150kB gz lighter index bundle once DotMatrix is gone).
     - CustomCursor TSX is structurally OK (refs, delegation, single rAF,
     transform3d) but: never-sleeping rAF, per-event object allocation,
     frame-rate-dependent lerp, useState-gated mount, and a brutal CSS module
     (ring backdrop-filter: blur(6px), bloom filter: blur(80px) animated via 
     keyframes = continuous repaint, .enlarged resizes via width/height/margins,
     3 full-screen mix-blend-mode layers).
     - anime.js v4 API verified (context7, animejs.com): animate() targets plain
     JS objects; stagger(v, {grid:[c,r], from: index, axis});
     createTimeline({autoplay:false}) + .seek(time, muteCallbacks?);
     svg.createDrawable() ‚Üí draw: '0 1'; utils.remove(targets, instance?, 
     prop?); createScope({mediaQueries}); engine.pauseOnDocumentHidden default
     true. Install animejs@^4 (current 4.3.x). v4.1+ text.split NOT used (we
     ship our own server-rendered splitter).

     Hard constraints

     - NO ResizeObserver anywhere (codebase law). Triggers =
     IntersectionObserver; scrubbing = Lenis callback / FM useScroll; resizes =
     existing resizeCoordinator. Do NOT use anime's onScroll (unverified
     internals re: RO).
     - No shrinkwrap on centered text; Pretext-wrapped text animates as whole
     blocks (opacity/transform) only ‚ÄĒ per-char splitting is reserved for
     headings the page owns directly.
     - Static export: all motion code 'use client', zero window/document at
     module scope.
     - One animation owner per element property ‚ÄĒ FM and anime never write the
     same node.

       'cubicBezier(0.25, 1, 0.5, 1)' (not the 'outQuart' approximation)

     2. Fonts ‚ÄĒ src/fonts/

     4. Motion system ‚ÄĒ src/lib/motion/

     4.1 Ownership (one owner per element)

     - anime.js v4: DotGrid values, ScrollTrace timeline, per-char/word/line
     text reveals, decode/scramble, typewriter, counters, logo disassemble,
     Konami boot, letter-roll links.
     - Framer Motion: AnimatePresence (dropdown/mobile menu/overlay exits),
     layoutId nav underline, whileInView card entrances (existing idiom + mock),
     whileTap squash, useScroll (progress bar, scroll-cue fade).
     - Raw rAF lerp: CustomCursor engine, useMagnetic.
     - CSS only: all simple hovers (brackets, underline grows, gradient sweeps,
     blink, scanlines).
     - Lenis: the single scroll driver (window-native, so IO + FM useScroll Just
     Work); useLenis for scrollTo on nav clicks; stop()/start() for overlays;
     ScrollTrace subscribes directly.

     4.2 Files

     tokens.ts (EASE arrays/strings, DUR, STAGGER, spring presets;
     src/utils/animations.ts becomes a re-export shim), anime.ts (sole animejs
     import point ‚Üí one-line vitest mock), useMotionPreference.ts (module-level
     matchMedia store via useSyncExternalStore + non-hook getter; every
     primitive skips-to-final-state under reduced motion; cursor consumes it
     too), useAnimeScope.ts (createScope({root, mediaQueries}) + revert()
     cleanup), useInViewOnce.ts (shared-IO map, mirrors resizeCoordinator
     pattern), splitText.tsx + RevealText.tsx (server-rendered span splitter ‚ÄĒ
     no hydration shift, no FOUC; masked rise y: 110%‚Üí0), useMagnetic.ts,
     colorRamp.ts, dotGridGeometry.ts, scrollTracePath.ts (pure, unit-tested),
     index.ts barrel with the ownership-rules doc comment.

     FOUC guard: tiny inline script in <head> sets data-loading on <html>; CSS
     hides hero/header entrance targets under it; LoadSequence removes it as the
     timeline starts; <noscript> + 2.5s failsafe ensure content can never stay
     hidden.

     4.3 Load sequence (one anime timeline, ~1.4s)

     Header logo + nav stagger(60) rise ‚Üí eyebrow decode (450ms scramble
     resolve) ‚Üí 3 headline masked line-rises 750ms stagger(90), line 3 gradient
     background-position sweep ‚Üí description block fade/rise (whole
     PretextBlock) ‚Üí CTAs stagger(80), arrow does a one-time 6px wink ‚Üí DotGrid
     corner entrance (¬ß5) + one qubetx:pulse beat from bottom-right ("system
     online").

     4.4 SectionHeading system (consistent across all 6 sections)

     Pill fade + char decode (cycle !<>-_\/[]{}‚ÄĒ=+*^?#, resolve L‚ÜíR, 450ms) ‚Üí h2
     RevealText mode="words" masked rise 600ms stagger(40) ‚Üí hairline scaleX
     700ms overlapping. Trigger: useInViewOnce 0.6. Reduced motion: static.

     5. DotGrid ‚ÄĒ the anime.js hero field (replaces R3F DotMatrix)

     Substrate: Canvas 2D blitter, anime.js owns 100% of animated values
     (animates a flat array of plain dot objects ‚ÄĒ verified API). DOM divs at
     ~800 nodes = 5-9ms/frame style recalc; SVG worse (no compositor promotion);
     canvas = ~0.3-0.8ms anime tick + ~1-1.5ms batched arc paint at DPR ‚Č§1.5.
     "Fully anime.js" holds: anime is the engine, canvas just draws.

     - Scope: hero right ~55% only (~28px pitch ‚Üí ~670-790 dots). Page-wide
     continuity via the static CSS dot texture (¬ß1). One animated background at
     a time (ScrollTrace owns the rest of the page).
     - Model: {x, y, baseR(1.0‚Üí2.6px), baseA(0.12‚Üí0.55), baseMix(0‚Üí1 along TL‚ÜíBR
     diagonal), breathe, pulse, alpha, mix}. Static ramp = the mockup's
     grow/brighten-toward-bottom-right. Color via 256-entry #0066FF‚Üí#7c3aed LUT
     (no per-frame color math).
     - Audit correction (mine): idle and ripple animate separate channels ‚ÄĒ idle
     loop owns breathe (scale 1‚Üí1.16‚Üí1, alpha shimmer, 3400ms, stagger(45, 
     {grid, from:'center'}), loop), ripples own pulse/mix. Render radius = baseR
     * breathe * pulse. Ripples never have to kill the idle loop;
     utils.remove(dots, undefined, 'pulse') only clears prior ripples.
     - Entrance: createTimeline().add(dots, {scale/alpha from 0, 600ms, 
     'out(3)', delay: stagger(10, {grid:[cols,rows], from: cols*rows-1})}) ‚ÄĒ
     sweeps in from the bottom-right corner.
     - Pointer ripple: hero-wrapper pointermove (passive, canvas
     pointer-events:none), throttled ‚Č•24px-or-90ms, reused point object ‚Üí
     nearestDotIndex (pure math) ‚Üí pulse: [{to: 2.2, 160ms, 'out(2)'}, {to: 1, 
     520ms, 'outElastic(1,.6)'}] + mix flash, delay: stagger(9, {grid, from: 
     idx}). pointerleave ‚Üí ease back to baseline.
     - External trigger bus: window CustomEvent qubetx:pulse {x, y, strength} ‚Üí
     ripple from given origin. Used by load sequence, typing egg, logo
     snap-back.
     - Lifecycle: own rAF draw loop; IO on hero pauses draw + idleAnim.pause()
     offscreen; engine.pauseOnDocumentHidden covers hidden tabs; resize via
     resizeCoordinator (rebuild geometry, 0-duration re-entrance); unmount =
     utils.remove(dots) + cancel rAF + IO disconnect. Reduced motion
     (createScope mediaQueries): draw the static ramp once, no loop, no ripples.
     SSR: empty <canvas> server-side, CSS-sized.

     6. ScrollTrace ‚ÄĒ scroll-scrubbed draw (down = draw, up = undraw)

     Concept: circuit trace with isometric cube junction nodes ‚ÄĒ one continuous
     PCB-style path descending the left gutter (mirrored right segment ‚Č•1440px),
     45¬į jogs, passing through a small wireframe cube node at each section
     boundary that assembles as the trace head reaches it. On-brand trifecta:
     infrastructure (circuit), logo (cubes), dot-matrix (dots at vias).

     - Layer: absolutely-positioned full-document SVG inside relative <main>
     (fixed can't weave past content), pointer-events:none aria-hidden, z
     between dot texture and content. Geometry from scrollTracePath.ts (pure):
     section anchor y-offsets measured once (getBoundingClientRect().top + 
     scrollY), re-measured via resizeCoordinator + once after Pretext fonts
     settle. X clamped to gutters (24px‚Ä¶~140px); display:none <1024px (gutters
     too thin ‚ÄĒ correct, not a regression).
     - Scrub: paused createTimeline({autoplay:false}) of svg.createDrawable
     segments (draw: ['0 0','0 1'], durations ‚ąĚ segment length, cube-node edges
     + dim opacity at junction positions). Driven by useLenis((lenis) => 
     tl.seek(lenis.progress * tl.duration)) ‚ÄĒ same-frame sync with the smoothed
     value the eye sees; seek() is bidirectional so reversal is free. (Chosen
     over anime onScroll: avoids double-smoothing/phase-lag between two rAF
     consumers, and sidesteps the RO question entirely.)
     - Style: stroke 1.5px, url(#traceGradient) blue‚Üípurple userSpaceOnUse,
     opacity 0.3; cheap glow = second pass of same d, wider stroke, opacity
     0.06. No SVG filters ever (per-frame repaint trap). Reduced motion: full
     trace static at 0.15.

     7. CustomCursor ‚ÄĒ same look, real engine

     cursorEngine.ts ‚ÄĒ framework-free class (unit-testable: stub divs, manual
     tick(dt), assert transform strings). CustomCursor.tsx = thin mount, no 
     React state; divs render always, CSS hides on hover:none; reduced-motion
     via shared store.

     - Single rAF; transform-only writes with centering folded in:
     translate3d(x,y,0) translate(-50%,-50%) rotate(őł) scale(1+s, 1/(1+s)) ‚ÄĒ
     velocity-aligned squash/stretch (s = clamp(speed¬∑0.0045, 0, .35), őł = 
     atan2(vy,vx)); cash.app physicality.
     - Delta-time-normalized lerp (my addition ‚ÄĒ agent missed it): k' = 1 ‚ąí 
     (1‚ąík)^(dt¬∑60) so trailing feel is identical at 60/120/144Hz. Factors stay
     0.32 ring / 0.22 bloom.
     - Settle detection: deltas < 0.05px + no pending mode change ‚Üí cancel rAF;
     resume on pointermove. Idle cost: zero (today it runs forever).
     - Delegated pointerover/out/down/up on document + pointermove on window,
     all passive; mode via closest(): [data-magnetic] > interactive > text.
     Press: scale‚Üí0.85 fast lerp, release overshoot 1.06 (6-line
     critically-damped settle). Magnetic mode: ring docks toward the element
     center (rect cached on enter, refreshed on Lenis scroll while hovered),
     border-radius morphs to the target's; dot keeps tracking the true pointer.
     - CSS module fixes: delete ring backdrop-filter; bloom's pre-blurred static
     gradient with opacity-only keyframes (never animate filter); .enlarged ‚Üí
     --cursor-scale consumed in the transform write (no width/height/margin);
     animation-play-state: paused while hidden; will-change: transform on
     exactly these 3 layers.

     8. Micro-interaction catalog (cash.app-derived: intentional / effortless / 
     organic)

     1. Button squash-stretch: FM whileTap scaleX 1.04 / scaleY 0.92, release
     spring 600/18 with ~1.03 overshoot ‚ÄĒ GET STARTED (header + hero), Contact
     CTA, back-to-top.
     2. OutlineButton hover: gradient layer sweep background-position 100%‚Üí0 +
     label flip 350ms --ease-out; arrow exits/re-enters through a clipped 1px
     gap.
     3. Letter-roll links (RollingLink.tsx): two stacked copies per char in
     overflow-hidden span; y: -100%, 420ms 'out(4)', stagger(18), utils.remove
     before reverse ‚ÄĒ nav links, footer links, "Visit Site ‚Üó".
     4. Cursor-proximity glow: one passive pointermove on each card grid
     container sets --mx/--my; card ::before radial gradient follows ‚ÄĒ reacts
     ~80px before hover (proximity, not hover). CSS + 1 listener, no lib.
     5. Magnetic pull (useMagnetic): 6px CTA / 4px logo, lerp 0.18 while
     engaged, spring-back overshoot; pairs with cursor docking via
     [data-magnetic].
     6. Card lift + micro-tilt: project cards only ‚ÄĒ FM hover y:-6, rotateX/Y
     ‚Č§3.5¬į from cached rect, spring 260/22; service/product rows get lift + glow
     only (restraint where rows are wide).
     7. Icon nudge: service icons rotate [0,-10,8,0] + scale 1.12, 600ms
     'outElastic(1,.5)' on card hover.
     8. Scroll progress: 2px top bar, --gradient-brand, FM scaleX MotionValue
     (zero re-renders).

     9. Easter eggs (one lazy EasterEggProvider, single multiplexed keydown 
     ring-buffer; ignores inputs/textareas/contentEditable)

     1. Konami code ‚Üí TR-300 WEB REPORT (hero egg): next/dynamic full-screen
     role="dialog" terminal overlay (scanline CSS); lenis.stop(); anime timeline
     boot-prints a machine-report-style diagnostic of the site itself ‚ÄĒ HOST: 
     qubetx.com / OS: shaughvOS / FRAMEWORK: next@16 react@19 / RENDER: STATIC 
     EXPORT / DOT GRID: ~780 NODES [OK] / CPU CORES: 
     navigator.hardwareConcurrency / VIEWPORT / FPS (sampled) ‚Ä¶ ALL SYSTEMS 
     NOMINAL, final line links to reports.qubetx.com. Line stagger 90ms, char
     stagger 14ms, green OK flashes. ESC closes with CRT power-off exit
     (scaleY‚Üí0.005 then scaleX‚Üí0). Reduced motion: instant-print variant.
     Discoverability: footer glyph + console hint.
     2. Typing qubetx ‚Üí qubetx:pulse shockwave from viewport center through
     DotGrid + 1.2s hue swing toward purple and back. Cheap (reuses ¬ß5 bus),
     repeatable, satisfying.
     3. Logo click-spam (5√ó in 2.5s) ‚Üí cube disassemble: anime timeline on
     QubeTXLogo's data-face groups (needs forwardRef + group ids) ‚ÄĒ faces
     translate/rotate outward stagger(40, {from:'center'}), strokes un-draw 30%
     via createDrawable, hold, spring reassemble (createSpring 160/12) + small
     qubetx:pulse at logo position. Locked while running.
     4. Console signature: styled ASCII cube, %cQUBETX // SYSTEMS NOMINAL,
     recruiting line, hints for #1/#2. Runs once on mount.
     5. (Stretch ‚ÄĒ cut first) 60s idle ‚Üí dots drift into a cube-outline
     formation (anime animates dot x/y toward precomputed targets ‚ÄĒ easier on
     canvas than the old shader idea), any input scatters them back.

     10. Performance & a11y budget

     Steady-state main thread: DotGrid ~1ms idle / ‚Č§2.3ms rippling (0
     offscreen), cursor 0 idle / <0.2ms moving, ScrollTrace ~0.4ms per scroll
     frame (0 still), micro-interactions transient. Worst case <4ms ‚ÄĒ headroom
     beside Lenis + React. Listeners passive; pointermove
     distance/time-throttled; will-change: transform only on 3 cursor layers; no
     SVG/canvas filters; no backdrop-filter except the header bar; anime
     timelines all finite (idle engine empty ‚ÄĒ verify in devtools). Bundle:
     +animejs subset ~12-18kB gz, ‚ąíR3F/three off the index route (~150kB gz) ‚Üí
     net lighter. KonamiTerminal + disassemble code-split. A11y: all motion
     behind useMotionPreference (skip-to-final, not slower); focus management in
     dropdown/mobile menu/overlay; aria-expanded everywhere; keyboard path for
     everything pointer does; WCAG AA contrast on dim text (#64748b on #05070f ‚Čą
     4.6:1 ‚úď).

      30 +/** Minimal MotionValue stub for useScroll/useTransform consume
         +rs. */                                                         
      31 +class MockMotionValue<T = number> {                            
      32 +  private listeners = new Set<(v: T) => void>()                
      33 +  constructor(private value: T) {}                             
      34 +  get = () => this.value                                       
      35 +  set = (v: T) => {                                            
      36 +    this.value = v                                             
      37 +    this.listeners.forEach((l) => l(v))                        
      38 +  }                                                            
      39 +  on = (_event: string, cb: (v: T) => void) => {               
      40 +    this.listeners.add(cb)                                     
      41 +    return () => this.listeners.delete(cb)                     
      42 +  }                                                            
      43 +  destroy = () => this.listeners.clear()                       
      44 +}                                                              
      45 +                                                               
      46 +export const useMotionValue = <T,>(initial: T) => new MockMotio
         +nValue(initial)                                                
      47 +export const useScroll = () => ({                              
      48 +  scrollX: new MockMotionValue(0),                             
      49 +  scrollY: new MockMotionValue(0),                             
      50 +  scrollXProgress: new MockMotionValue(0),                     
      51 +  scrollYProgress: new MockMotionValue(0),                     
      52 +})                                                             
      53 +export const useTransform = () => new MockMotionValue(0)       
      54 +export const useSpring = (v: unknown) =>                       
      55 +  v instanceof MockMotionValue ? v : new MockMotionValue(v as n
         +umber)                                                         
      56 +export const useMotionValueEvent = () => {}                    
      57 +export const useReducedMotion = () => false

         +server {                                                       
      27 +  static instances: MockIntersectionObserver[] = []            
      28 +  readonly root: Element | Document | null = null

         +bserverEntry

         +, CSS vars

         +eps FM's                                                       
      18 +  // entrance variants ‚ÄĒ different node, no shared transform). 
      19 +  const rectRef = useRef<DOMRect | null>(null)

      24 +    rafRef.current = null                                      
      25 +    const rect = rectRef.current                               
      26 +    if (!rect) return

      30 +    el.style.setProperty('--rx', `${(-py * MAX_TILT * 2).toFixe

         +text splitter + masked reveals, magnetic pull, proximity glow ‚ÄĒ
         + with strict per-element ownership rules (anime / Framer Motion
         + / raw rAF / CSS)

         + (Canvas 2D blitter; breathe/pulse channels; distance-delay rip
         +ples; feathered edges dissolving into the next section; `qubetx
         +:pulse` event bus)

         +ebrow scramble-decode ‚Üí masked headline rises ‚Üí gradient sweep 
         +‚Üí CTAs ‚Üí "system online" pulse) with an inline-script FOUC guar
         +d

         + cube junctions ‚ÄĒ draws scrolling down, reverses scrolling up (
         +paused timeline + Lenis seek)

       78 -### Pretext Integration (`src/lib/pretext/`)                  
       79 +## Motion System ‚ÄĒ LOAD-BEARING RULES                         
       80  
       80 -The site uses `@chenglou/pretext` for JS-driven text measureme
          -nt beneath the CSS responsive design. Pretext provides two cap
          -abilities: **layout-shift prevention** (reserving exact text h
          -eight via `min-height`) and **orphan/widow prevention** (narro
          -wing `max-width` via binary-search shrinkwrap).               
       81 +Full specs in `DESIGN_SYSTEM.md` ¬ß5. The short version every c
          +hange must obey:                                              
       82  
       82 -```                                                           
       83 -src/lib/pretext/                                              
       84 -‚Ēú‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ resizeCoordinator.ts  # Single global window.resize listen
          -er + RAF gate                                                 
       85 -‚Ēú‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ useContainerWidth.ts  # Sync clientWidth measurement hook 
          -(NO ResizeObserver)                                           
       86 -‚Ēú‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ PretextProvider.tsx   # Font readiness context (document.f
          -onts.ready)                                                   
       87 -‚Ēú‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ PretextBlock.tsx      # Drop-in wrapper: min-height + shri
          -nkwrap max-width                                              
       88 -‚Ēú‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ index.ts              # Barrel export                     
       89 -‚ĒĒ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ __tests__/            # Unit tests for coordinator and pro
          -vider                                                         
       90 -```                                                           
       83 +1. **One animation owner per element property.** anime.js owns
          + dot values,                                                  
       84 +   timelines, text reveals; Framer Motion owns presence/layout
          +/whileTap/                                                    
       85 +   useScroll; raw rAF owns cursor/magnetic/tilt; CSS owns simp
          +le hovers.                                                    
       86 +   An FM-variant element is never also an anime target.       
       87 +2. **NO ResizeObserver anywhere** (Pretext law ‚ÄĒ causes shrink
          +wrap                                                          
       88 +   oscillation). Resizes go through `src/lib/pretext/resizeCoo
          +rdinator`.                                                    
       89 +   Scroll triggers = IntersectionObserver (`useInViewOnce`); s
          +crubbing =                                                    
       90 +   Lenis callbacks. anime's `onScroll` is banned.             
       91 +3. **Reduced motion = skip to final state**, never slower     
       92 +   (`useMotionPreference` / `prefersReducedMotion()`).        
       93 +4. anime.js is imported ONLY via `src/lib/motion/anime.ts` (th
          +e test-mock seam).                                            
       94 +5. Anchor navigation goes through `useAnchorNav` (Lenis scroll
          +To); CSS                                                      
       95 +   `scroll-behavior: smooth` is intentionally absent.         
       96 +6. Server HTML always shows FINAL state (visible text); hidden
          +/initial states                                               
       97 +   are applied client-side (LoadSequence/RevealText), guarded 
          +against FOUC by                                               
       98 +   the `html[data-loading]` inline script (3s failsafe).      
       99  
       92 -**Critical Rules:**                                           
       93 -- **NEVER use ResizeObserver** with Pretext ‚ÄĒ causes text vibr
          -ation/oscillation with shrinkwrap. Confirmed across multiple p
          -rojects after two failed attempts. The correct pattern: sync `
          -clientWidth` reads + `window.resize` coalesced through a singl
          -e RAF gate.                                                   
       94 -- **NEVER use `shrinkwrap` on centered text** ‚ÄĒ shrinkwrap nar
          -rows `max-width`, which conflicts with `text-align: center` + 
          -`margin: 0 auto`, pulling text off-center. Centered elements (
          -section subtitles) should use PretextBlock for `min-height` on
          -ly.                                                           
       95 -- PretextBlock reads font properties from `getComputedStyle()`
          - to handle `next/font/google` rewritten names (e.g. `"__Unboun
          -ded_a1b2c3"`)                                                 
       96 -- `prepare()` is re-called only when resolved font size change
          -s >0.5px (for `clamp()` values)                               
       97 -- All enhancements are additive (`min-height`, narrower `max-w
          -idth`) and gracefully degrade if fonts aren't loaded          
       98 -- Package ships raw `.ts` source ‚ÄĒ requires `transpilePackages
          -` in next.config and `allowImportingTsExtensions` in tsconfig 
      100 +## Pretext Integration (`src/lib/pretext/`)                   
      101  
      100 -**PretextBlock props:**                                       
      101 -- `text` (string) ‚ÄĒ plain text content to measure             
      102 -- `lineHeight` (number) ‚ÄĒ unitless ratio matching CSS `line-he
          -ight`                                                         
      103 -- `shrinkwrap` (boolean) ‚ÄĒ enable orphan/widow prevention via 
          -`max-width` narrowing (only for left-aligned text)            
      104 -- `as` (ElementType) ‚ÄĒ rendered HTML element (defaults to `div
          -`)                                                            
      105 -- `className`, `style` ‚ÄĒ pass-through styling                 
      102 +Unchanged core rules (confirmed across many projects):        
      103  
      107 -**Usage patterns:**                                           
      108 -```tsx                                                        
      109 -{/* Left-aligned paragraph ‚ÄĒ use shrinkwrap for orphan prevent
          -ion */}                                                       
      110 -<PretextBlock text={description} lineHeight={1.65} shrinkwrap 
          -as="p" className={styles.description}>                        
      111 -  {description}                                               
      112 -</PretextBlock>                                               
      104 +- **NEVER use ResizeObserver** with Pretext ‚ÄĒ sync `clientWidt
          +h` reads +                                                    
      105 +  `window.resize` coalesced through one RAF gate (`resizeCoord
          +inator`).                                                     
      106 +- **NEVER `shrinkwrap` centered text** (narrowed `max-width` b
          +reaks centering).                                             
      107 +  Left-aligned text: `shrinkwrap` welcome. Centered: `min-heig
          +ht` only.                                                     
      108 +- **Never measure letter-spaced text** (mono pills/eyebrows/na
          +v) ‚ÄĒ canvas                                                   
      109 +  measurement ignores `letter-spacing`.                       
      110 +- Pretext-wrapped text animates as whole blocks only (opacity/
          +transform).                                                   
      111 +- `PretextBlock` reads `getComputedStyle()` (handles next/font
          + rewritten                                                    
      112 +  names). `PretextProvider` resolves **computed** family names
          + for its                                                      
      113 +  readiness check ‚ÄĒ literal names never match under next/font.
      114 +- Advanced APIs in play: `RoutedText` uses `prepareWithSegment
          +s` +                                                          
      115 +  `layoutNextLine` to flow the About lead paragraph around the
          + cube.                                                        
      116 +- Package ships raw `.ts` ‚Üí `transpilePackages` in next.config
          + +                                                            
      117 +  `allowImportingTsExtensions` in tsconfig.                   
      118  
      114 -{/* Centered subtitle ‚ÄĒ NO shrinkwrap (conflicts with centerin
          -g) */}                                                        
      115 -<PretextBlock text={subtitle} lineHeight={1.6} as="p" classNam
          -e={styles.sectionSubtitle}>                                   
      116 -  {subtitle}                                                  
      117 -</PretextBlock>                                               
      119 +## Testing

      119 -{/* Short title ‚ÄĒ min-height only, no shrinkwrap needed */}

          -{styles.title}>                                               
      121 -  {title}                                                     
      122 -</PretextBlock>

      133 +## Project Learnings & Decisions (v3 redesign ‚ÄĒ keep these)   
      134  
      127 -### Data Layer                                                
      135 +1. **anime.js 4.4 removed string cubic-bezier easings** ‚ÄĒ impo
          +rt the                                                        
      136 +   `cubicBezier` function (wrapped as `EASE_ANIME` in `lib/mot
          +ion/tokens`).                                                 
      137 +   The old string form silently warned 1300√ó/load and fell bac
          +k to default.                                                 
      138 +2. **Hydration**: never initialize React state from browser-AP
          +I presence                                                    
      139 +   (`typeof IntersectionObserver === 'undefined'` is TRUE in N
          +ode ‚Üí server                                                  
      140 +   HTML diverges). The FOUC-guard attribute on `<html>` requir
          +es                                                            
      141 +   `suppressHydrationWarning`.                                
      142 +3. **react-hooks v7 lint**: no sync `setState` inside effects 
          +(defer via                                                    
      143 +   rAF); no ref reads during render (`useMemo` instead).      
      144 +4. **Container queries** size the hero headline (`8cqw`, longe
          +st line is                                                    
      145 +   ~12.2em of Makira Black) ‚ÄĒ the only way to guarantee single
          +-line fit to a                                                
      146 +   column. `--text-display` (vw clamp) is kept as the no-CQ fa
          +llback.                                                       
      147 +5. **DotGrid optimization model**: anime animates plain JS obj
          +ects; canvas                                                  
      148 +   only blits. Feathered geometry CULLS invisible dots; all de
          +lays are                                                      
      149 +   distance functions (not grid staggers) so culling is safe; 
          +idle vs ripple                                                
      150 +   tweens live on separate channels (`breathe` vs `pulse`/`mix
          +`).                                                           
      151 +6. **CSS animations beat inline styles** ‚ÄĒ never animate a pro
          +perty an engine                                               
      152 +   writes inline on the same node. **Inline `display` beats me
          +dia queries** ‚ÄĒ                                               
      153 +   wrappers (Magnetic) set display via class.                 
      154 +7. **SVG groups with attribute matrices** must not receive tra
          +nsforms                                                       
      155 +   (CSS transform replaces the matrix) ‚ÄĒ animate strokes via  
      156 +   `svg.createDrawable` or the root `<svg>`.                  
      157 +8. **`--color-text-dim` (#76869f) is contrast-tuned** (‚Č•4.5:1 
          +AA on void) ‚ÄĒ                                                 
      158 +   don't darken. Touch-target 44px minimums apply under       
      159 +   `@media (pointer: coarse)` only.                           
      160 +9. **TV tier**: `--container-max` 1440px ‚Üí 1800px at ‚Č•2560px; 
          +everything                                                    
      161 +   (sections, cqw headline, ScrollTrace gutter) derives from t
          +he token.                                                     
      162 +10. **`qubetx:pulse` CustomEvent** is the dot-field's external
          + trigger bus                                                  
      163 +    (load beat, typing egg, logo egg) ‚ÄĒ reuse it rather than r
          +eaching into                                                  
      164 +    DotGrid.                                                  
      165 +11. Lighthouse at ship: 100 a11y / 100 best-practices / 100 SE
          +O;                                                            
      166 +    real-navigation CLS 0.000. Keep it that way.              
      167  
      129 -- `src/data/content.ts` - Centralized content data with TypeSc
          -ript types                                                    
      130 -  - Export typed constants: `HERO_CONTENT`, `FEATURES`, `PROJE
          -CTS`, `CONTACT_CTA`                                           
      131 -  - Single source of truth for all copy and content           
      132 -  - Types: `Feature`, `Project`, `HeroContent`, `ContactCta`  
      168 +## Common Gotchas                                             
      169  
      134 -### Styling Architecture                                      
      170 +1. This is **NOT** a Vite project ‚ÄĒ Next.js App Router, static
          + export.                                                      
      171 +2. Tailwind v4 `@theme` lives in `app/globals.css` (no config 
          +file); most                                                   
      172 +   styling is CSS Modules with the `--ease-out` / token vars. 
      173 +3. Static export: no ISR/API routes; images unoptimized.      
      174 +4. Build output is `out/` (Vercel serves it; no GitHub Pages a
          +nymore).                                                      
      175 +5. Display text is stored in sentence case ‚ÄĒ UPPERCASE is `tex
          +t-transform`.                                                 
      176 +6. The dev server may warn about a stray lockfile workspace ro
          +ot ‚ÄĒ harmless,                                                
      177 +   machine-level issue.                                       
      178 +7. R3F/three types: `src/r3f.d.ts` + `// @ts-nocheck` only ins
          +ide                                                           
      179 +   `WallpaperMatrix`.                                         
      180  
      136 -**Tailwind CSS v4 with @theme syntax:**                       
      137 -                                                              
      138 -- Global styles in `app/globals.css` using `@import "tailwindc
          -ss"`                                                          
      139 -- Theme configuration via `@theme` directive (not traditional 
          -config file)                                                  
      140 -- Custom CSS variables defined in `:root` for backward compati
          -bility                                                        
      141 -- Font variables injected from Next.js font optimization      
      142 -- No separate `tailwind.config.ts` - configuration in CSS via 
          -`@theme`                                                      
      143 -                                                              
      144 -**Key styling patterns:**                                     
      145 -- Utility-first with Tailwind classes                         
      146 -- CSS variables for legacy design system values               
      147 -- Custom animations defined in globals.css (`ambientPulse`, `a
          -uroraShift`)                                                  
      148 -- Responsive design with Tailwind breakpoints                 
      149 -- Custom cursor hidden via CSS on touch devices (`@media (poin
          -ter: fine)`)                                                  
      150 -                                                              
      151 -### React Three Fiber Integration                             
      152 -                                                              
      153 -`DotMatrix.tsx` creates an interactive 3D dot grid:           
      154 -- Uses `@react-three/fiber` Canvas and hooks                  
      155 -- Instanced mesh rendering for performance (2500 dots)        
      156 -- Mouse interaction via `useThree` hook                       
      157 -- Wave animation with `useFrame`                              
      158 -- Wrapped in Suspense for progressive loading                 
      159 -                                                              
      160 -**Important:** R3F components use `// @ts-nocheck` due to type
          - complexity. Type definitions in `src/r3f.d.ts`.              
      161 -                                                              
      162 -## Build Configuration                                        
      163 -                                                              
      164 -### next.config.mjs                                           
      165 -                                                              
      166 -```javascript                                                 
      167 -output: 'export'           // Static export for GitHub Pages  
      168 -images: { unoptimized: true }  // No Next.js image optimizatio
          -n                                                             
      169 -```                                                           
      170 -                                                              
      171 -### TypeScript Configuration                                  
      172 -                                                              
      173 -- **Module Resolution**: `bundler` (Next.js 16 default)       
      174 -- **JSX**: `react-jsx` (automatic runtime)                    
      175 -- **Path Alias**: `@/*` ‚Üí `./src/*`                           
      176 -- **Target**: ES2017                                          
      177 -- **Strict mode enabled**                                     
      178 -                                                              
      179 -### PostCSS Configuration                                     
      180 -                                                              
      181 -Uses Tailwind CSS v4 PostCSS plugin:                          
      182 -```javascript                                                 
      183 -"@tailwindcss/postcss": {}                                    
      184 -```                                                           
      185 -                                                              
      181  ## Design System
      182  
      188 -Follows specifications in `QubeTX_Design_System.md`:          
      189 -                                                              
      190 -### Typography                                                
      191 -- **Unbounded**: Headlines and titles (next/font/google)      
      192 -- **Space Grotesk**: Body text (next/font/google)             
      193 -- **Space Mono**: Technical text and tags (next/font/google)  
      194 -                                                              
      195 -### Color System                                              
      196 -- Primary Blue: `#0066FF`                                     
      197 -- Dark Background: `#0a0f1c`                                  
      198 -- Card Background: `#0d1117`                                  
      199 -- Gradient Blue: `#2563eb`                                    
      200 -- Gradient Purple: `#7c3aed`                                  
      201 -                                                              
      202 -### Grid System                                               
      203 -- 8px base unit (`--grid-unit`)                               
      204 -- Responsive spacing with CSS clamp() functions               
      205 -- Mobile-first breakpoints: 375px, 390px, 414px, 768px, 1200px
      206 -- Touch target minimum: 44px                                  
      207 -                                                              
      208 -## CI/CD Pipeline                                             
      209 -                                                              
      210 -GitHub Actions workflow (`.github/workflows/ci.yml`):         
      211 -                                                              
      212 -1. **build-and-test** - Type check, run tests, build, upload a
          -rtifacts                                                      
      213 -2. **deploy-preview** - Preview deployments for PRs           
      214 -3. **deploy-production** - Auto-deploy to GitHub Pages on main
          - branch push                                                  
      215 -4. **code-quality** - Security audit, bundle size reporting   
      216 -5. **notify** - Build status notifications                    
      217 -                                                              
      218 -**Important:** The build outputs to `out/` directory (not `dis
          -t/`). CI uses `npm test` which must be configured.            
      219 -                                                              
      220 -## Deployment                                                 
      221 -                                                              
      222 -- **Platform**: GitHub Pages                                  
      223 -- **Trigger**: Push to main branch                            
      224 -- **Process**: Automated via GitHub Actions                   
      225 -- **Custom Domain**: Configured via `public/CNAME`            
      226 -- **Build Artifacts**: Static export in `out/` directory      
      227 -                                                              
      228 -## Key Implementation Details                                 
      229 -                                                              
      230 -### Font Loading                                              
      231 -Fonts are loaded via Next.js `next/font/google` in `app/layout
          -.tsx`:                                                        
      232 -- Creates CSS variables (`--font-unbounded`, `--font-space-gro
          -tesk`, `--font-space-mono`)                                   
      233 -- Applied to body via className with `.variable`              
      234 -- Optimized with `display: "swap"`                            
      235 -                                                              
      236 -### Custom Cursor                                             
      237 -- Only active on devices with `pointer: fine` (non-touch)     
      238 -- Global cursor disabled via CSS in globals.css               
      239 -- Magnetic attraction to interactive elements                 
      240 -- Respects `prefers-reduced-motion`                           
      241 -- Layered design with bloom, ring, and core elements          
      242 -                                                              
      243 -### Smooth Scrolling                                          
      244 -- Implemented via Lenis library                               
      245 -- Client component wrapping app content                       
      246 -- Disabled on touch devices for native feel                   
      247 -                                                              
      248 -### Static Assets                                             
      249 -- Located in `public/` directory                              
      250 -- Referenced as `/filename.png` in code                       
      251 -- Includes: logos, project images, favicon, CNAME             
      252 -                                                              
      253 -## Common Gotchas                                             
      254 -                                                              
      255 -1. **This is NOT a Vite project** - It's Next.js with App Rout
          -er                                                            
      256 -2. **Tailwind v4 syntax** - Uses `@theme` directive, not tradi
          -tional config                                                 
      257 -3. **Static export mode** - Some Next.js features unavailable 
          -(ISR, API routes)                                             
      258 -4. **Images unoptimized** - Next.js Image component works but 
          -without optimization                                          
      259 -5. **R3F type issues** - Use `// @ts-nocheck` for complex Thre
          -e.js typing                                                   
      260 -6. **Build output** - Goes to `out/` not `dist/` (some CI refe
          -rences still say `dist/`)                                     
      261 -7. **Port differences** - Dev server is port 3000 (Next.js def
          -ault), not 8080                                               
      262 -8. **Pretext ships raw .ts** - Requires `transpilePackages` an
          -d `allowImportingTsExtensions` ‚ÄĒ see Pretext Integration secti
          -on                                                            
      263 -9. **Pretext shrinkwrap + centering** - Never use `shrinkwrap`
          - on `text-align: center` elements ‚ÄĒ it breaks centering by nar
          -rowing `max-width`

          +m.md` is the

  What was built

  The mockup, realized ‚ÄĒ Makira Black three-line headline (gradient third line,
  container-query-sized so it never wraps on desktop), mono eyebrow with
  scramble-decode, outlined magnetic CTAs, centered mono nav with an accessible
  SERVICES dropdown, and the dot field ‚ÄĒ now fully Anime.js-driven (canvas is
  just the blitter): elastic ripples radiate from your cursor with
  distance-based delays, the field feathers to nothing on the left and dissolves
  ~26vh into the next section, per your notes.

  The rest of the page ‚ÄĒ terminal-flavored Products section (typed $ qubetx 
  --products boot line, striped rows for TR-300/SD-300/ND-300/WB-300/shaughvOS ‚Üí
  reports.qubetx.com), About with count-up stats (hover "re-verifies" them ‚ÄĒ
  numeral re-roll + label decode) and the Pretext showcase (the lead paragraph
  literally flows around a wireframe cube via layoutNextLine), Work grid with
  pointer micro-tilt, the scroll-scrubbed circuit trace that draws down the
  gutter through cube junctions and reverses when you scroll up, rebuilt cursor
  engine (zero idle cost, velocity squash/stretch, magnetic docking), and four
  themed Easter eggs ‚ÄĒ EASTER_EGGS.md in the repo root is your answer key (try
  the Konami code; the TR-300 WEB REPORT prints live diagnostics of your actual
  machine).

‚óŹ PowerShell(git add -A; git commit -m @'
            feat(services): LED dot-matrix display fills the empty grid space‚Ä¶)
  ‚éŅ ¬†warning: in the working copy of 'DESIGN_SYSTEM.md', LF will be replace

‚óŹ Done ‚ÄĒ that empty cell is now an LED dot-matrix display, exactly the
  Hermes-style treatment you described.

  What fills the space: a coarse dot board where Anime.js sweeps words across
  the grid in an endless loop ‚ÄĒ QUBETX ‚Üí BUILD ‚Üí SHIP ‚Üí SECURE ‚Üí SCALE ‚ÄĒ each
  transition staggered column-by-column left to right, with the dots colored
  along the brand blue‚Üípurple ramp and a faint unlit grid behind (proper
  LED-board feel). It follows the same architecture as the hero field: anime.js
  owns every animated value (each dot's lit channel), canvas only paints, it
  pauses offscreen, rebuilds on resize, and reduced-motion users get a static
  word.

  Two details worth knowing:

  - It adapts to whatever space is left. The Services grid now uses explicit
  column counts (1/2/3/4 across breakpoints), so at 4 columns the board spans
  the three empty tracks beside Security & Performance; at 2‚Äď3 columns it takes
  the single leftover cell; on mobile it becomes its own full-width band. The
  board's dot pitch derives from the longest word, so the glyphs always span
  roughly the full cell ‚ÄĒ chunky LEDs in the wide cell, finer dots in small
  ones. (First attempt used grid-column: auto / -1, which I caught in the
  screenshot resolving to a single track ‚ÄĒ that CSS footgun is now documented in
  DESIGN_SYSTEM.md.)
  - The 5√ó7 bitmap font is a pure, unit-tested module
  (src/lib/motion/dotFont.ts), so swapping the word list is a one-line change in
  Services.tsx (MATRIX_WORDS) ‚ÄĒ happy to change the words if you want different
  ones.

  Gate is green (34 files / 148 tests, lint, build) and it's committed on
  feature/redesign-v3. Take a look at localhost:3000 ‚ÄĒ if the cycle pacing or
  dot density feels off, those are single constants (HOLD_MS, SWEEP_MS,
  COL_PADDING) I can tune in seconds.
